{
 "cells": [
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "# A basic example\n",
    "\n",
    "The most basic usecase of TOPP-RA is compute the time-optimal\n",
    "time-parameterization subject to joint velocity and acceleration\n",
    "constraints. \n",
    "\n",
    "## Setup the problem\n",
    "\n",
    "First, we need to load `toppra`."
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 1,
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# toppra\n",
    "import toppra as ta\n",
    "import toppra.constraint as constraint\n",
    "import toppra.algorithm as algo\n",
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "# misc: for plotting and measuring time\n",
    "import matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n",
    "import time"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "We now randomly choose 5 waypoints and fit a cubic spline through\n",
    "all five to obtain a geometric path."
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 2,
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [
    {
     "name": "stdout",
     "output_type": "stream",
     "text": [
      "<toppra.interpolator.SplineInterpolator object at 0x7f2b5e015590>\n"
     ]
    }
   ],
   "source": [
    "# Random waypoints used to obtain a random geometric path. Here,\n",
    "# we use spline interpolation.\n",
    "dof = 6\n",
    "way_pts = np.random.randn(5, dof)\n",
    "path = ta.SplineInterpolator(np.linspace(0, 1, 5), way_pts)\n",
    "print(path)"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "Similarly, we choose a random set of velocity and acceleration constraints below.\n",
    "\n",
    "A constraint can have different `discretization_scheme`: `Interpolation` and `Collocation`.\n",
    "Generally, `Interpolation` leads to higher quality trajectory with a longer (slightly) computation time."
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 3,
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [
    {
     "name": "stdout",
     "output_type": "stream",
     "text": [
      "JointAccelerationConstraint(\n",
      "    Type: ConstraintType.CanonicalLinear\n",
      "    Discretization Scheme: DiscretizationType.Interpolation\n",
      "    Acceleration limit: \n",
      "      J1: [-1.50261013  1.50261013]\n",
      "      J2: [-1.64066688  1.64066688]\n",
      "      J3: [-1.07645284  1.07645284]\n",
      "      J4: [-1.20220314  1.20220314]\n",
      "      J5: [-0.13926235  0.13926235]\n",
      "      J6: [-1.56480046  1.56480046]\n",
      ")\n"
     ]
    }
   ],
   "source": [
    "# Create velocity bounds, then velocity constraint object\n",
    "vlim_ = np.random.rand(dof) * 20\n",
    "vlim = np.vstack((-vlim_, vlim_)).T\n",
    "# Create acceleration bounds, then acceleration constraint object\n",
    "alim_ = np.random.rand(dof) * 2\n",
    "alim = np.vstack((-alim_, alim_)).T\n",
    "pc_vel = constraint.JointVelocityConstraint(vlim)\n",
    "pc_acc = constraint.JointAccelerationConstraint(\n",
    "   alim, discretization_scheme=constraint.DiscretizationType.Interpolation)\n",
    "\n",
    "print(pc_acc)"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "Notice that in the above printout, we have 6 acceleration joint limits with `Interpolation` `discretization_scheme`.\n",
    "\n",
    "## Solve TOPP\n",
    "\n",
    "We now solve for the time-optimal path parametrization:"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 19,
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [
    {
     "name": "stdout",
     "output_type": "stream",
     "text": [
      "Parameterization time: 0.00753903388977 secs\n"
     ]
    }
   ],
   "source": [
    "t0 = time.time()\n",
    "# Setup a parametrization instance, then retime\n",
    "instance = algo.TOPPRA([pc_vel, pc_acc], path, solver_wrapper='seidel')\n",
    "jnt_traj, aux_traj, int_data = instance.compute_trajectory(0, 0, return_data=True)\n",
    "print(\"Parameterization time: {:} secs\".format(time.time() - t0))"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "There are muliple solver wrapper to choose from: `seidel`, `hotqpoases`, `cvxpy`, etc.\n",
    "In general you should choose `seidel` because it is much faster than `hotqpoases`. However,\n",
    "be warned that `seidel` can fail for ill-posed path parametrization instances. \n",
    "\n",
    "Below we solve\n",
    "the same problem using different solver wrappers and compare their speeds."
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 7,
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [
    {
     "name": "stdout",
     "output_type": "stream",
     "text": [
      "seidel              : comp. time 0.0079 secs: traj dur. 16.428990 sec\n",
      "hotqpoases          : comp. time 0.0249 secs: traj dur. 16.428990 sec\n",
      "cvxpy               : comp. time 1.4635 secs: traj dur. 16.428993 sec\n"
     ]
    }
   ],
   "source": [
    "for solver_wrapper in ['seidel', 'hotqpoases', 'cvxpy']:\n",
    "    t0 = time.time()\n",
    "    instance = algo.TOPPRA([pc_vel, pc_acc], path, solver_wrapper=solver_wrapper)\n",
    "    traj, _ = instance.compute_trajectory(0, 0)\n",
    "    print(\"{:20}: comp. time {:.4f} secs: traj dur. {:4f} sec\".format(solver_wrapper, time.time() - t0, traj.get_duration()))"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "## Inspect solution\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "The time-optimally retimed geometric path can be recovered easily."
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 6,
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [

    "ts_sample = np.linspace(0, jnt_traj.get_duration(), 100)\n",
    "qdds_sample = jnt_traj.evaldd(ts_sample)\n",
    "qds_sample = jnt_traj.evald(ts_sample)\n",
